**KROK 8: FAQ ROZSZERZONE (ADVANCED TROUBLESHOOTING)**

**Q: Co jeÅ›li mam alergiÄ™ pokarmowÄ…?**
A: Powiedz o tym PRZED wizytÄ…! KoreaÅ„skie matki potrafiÄ… przygotowaÄ‡ 15 alternatywnych daÅ„ w 2 godziny. But NEVER spring this information during dinner - that's like bringing emergency update during system deployment.

**Q: Czy mogÄ™ uÅ¼yÄ‡ widelca i noÅ¼a?**

**Q: Co jeÅ›li jestem wegetarianinem/veganem?**

**Q: Jak dÅ‚ugo trwa average Korean family dinner?**
A: 2-4 godziny minimum. To nie jest McDonald's drive-through. Przygotuj siÄ™ mentalnie na marathon, nie sprint. Battery life twojej social energy powinna byÄ‡ na max.

**Q: Co jeÅ›li nie mogÄ™ jeÅ›Ä‡ bardzo ostrego jedzenia?**

**Q: Co jeÅ›li popeÅ‚niÄ™ cultural mistake?**
A: Universal fix algorithm: UkÅ‚on + "ì£„ì†¡í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤" (joesonghamnida) + zapytaj o proper way + pokaÅ¼ genuine desire to learn. Korean families appreciate effort more than perfection.

**Q: Co jeÅ›li nie rozumiem po koreaÅ„sku?**
A: Normal situation. Family usually switches to English/Polish dla ciebie. But learn basic phrases: ì•ˆë…•í•˜ì„¸ìš” (hello), ê°ì‚¬í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤ (thank you), ì£„ì†¡í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤ (sorry), ë§›ìˆì–´ìš” (delicious). Shows respect and effort.

**Q: Co robiÄ‡ z small talk?**
A: Safe topics: praca, edukacja, kultura polska, plany na przyszÅ‚oÅ›Ä‡. Avoid: polityka, poprzednie zwiÄ…zki, finanse, controversial topics. Keep it neutral and respectful.

**EMERGENCY PROTOCOLS**

**12.1 Crisis management procedures:**
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# Emergency cultural crisis handler

    echo "Minor awkwardness detected"
    execute_smile_and_nod_protocol()
    increase_politeness_level()
}

crisis_level_2() {  
    echo "Moderate cultural violation"
    execute_immediate_apology()
    request_cultural_guidance()
}

crisis_level_3() {
    echo "Major disaster in progress"
    activate_emergency_humility_mode()
    call_girlfriend_for_immediate_translation()
    prepare_extended_apology_sequence()
}

crisis_level_4() {
    echo "DEFCON 1 - Relationship at risk"
    execute_full_cultural_surrender()
    request_family_meeting_restart()
    consider_professional_cultural_counseling()
}
```

